                                       — the `.oui` branch now renders a small `OuiFileView` wrapper using
                                       the same hook and card (with `m-6` to match the viewer's other
                                       states).

                                       **How parse failure / no-root is detected**
                                       I confirmed the contract in `@openuidev/react-lang`'s Renderer: it
                                       returns `null` whenever the parse result has no root, and its
                                       `onError` effect reports exactly those fatal cases as `code:
                                       "parse-exception"` ("Parser crashed: …") or `code: "parse-failed"`
                                       ("Code parsed but produced no renderable root component" / "Response
                                       could not be parsed as valid openui-lang"). So no-root is *not*
                                       silent — no separate empty-render detection was needed. The hook
                                       filters on those two codes specifically, because `source: "parser"`
                                       also carries non-fatal validation errors (unknown-component etc.)
                                       that coexist with a rendering root. Empty response produces no error,
                                       so the file-viewer's empty in-memory document stays clean.

                                       **What the card shows**
                                       `FileWarningIcon` + "Broken artifact {url}: {message}" in the app's
                                       destructive-tinted style (`border-destructive/50 bg-destructive/10
                                       text-destructive`, matching chat-bar's error tint). In the embed, the
                                       card replaces the preview chrome and the shader/Expand button is
                                       dropped (nothing to expand); the zero-height `GenerativeView` stays
                                       mounted in both hosts so a wiki hot-reload that fixes the file clears
                                       the card automatically (Renderer re-fires `onError` with `[]`).

                                       **Verification**
                                       - `npm run typecheck -w client` passes; client lint exits 0 (only
                                       pre-existing-class fast-refresh warnings); `vite build` to scratchpad
                                       succeeds.

2026-07-13 05:05:52  ASSISTANT:        Both issues are fixed, with the flash diagnosed from live measurement
                                       rather than guesswork:

                                       **The flashing — root cause found and fixed.** I instrumented the
                                       authoring pane with a MutationObserver and ran real generation/edit
                                       turns through the app. The static paths (full-page view, embeds) were
                                       completely quiet — the flash is a streaming problem: every `ui:delta`
                                       chunk that grows a `Content` statement's `html` prop makes React
                                       wholesale-reset that subtree via `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`, and since
                                       artifacts keep their CSS in a `<style>` block *inside* a Content
                                       statement, the style element was being destroyed and recreated on
                                       every chunk — the whole artifact flashed unstyled at chunk rate
                                       (measured: 99 nodes added / 93 removed in one small generation, with
                                       `-STYLE/+STYLE` on every chunk).

                                       The fix in `ContentComponent`: `<style>` blocks are split out of the
                                       html and rendered as persistent React `<style>` elements — their text
                                       updates in place in a single commit, so there's never an unstyled
                                       frame — and an unclosed mid-stream `<style>` tail is withheld
                                       entirely so half-streamed CSS can't render as visible page text.
                                       Re-measured on a live streaming edit: **style removals went from
                                       every-chunk to zero**, and the pr-502764 benchmark artifact still
                                       renders fully styled (its 9.5KB style block extracted correctly).

                                       **The empty display.** The blank authoring pane (confirmed by
                                       screenshot — stark white page) now shows a calm centered "Blank
                                       artifact — nothing here yet." in muted text. That hunk sits inside
                                       another agent's heavy in-flight App.tsx refactor and rides with their
                                       commit; the renderer fix is queued behind the gate watcher.

                                       Two things I observed but deliberately left alone: the remaining
                                       per-chunk churn is genuine content growth (streaming text appearing —
                                       expected UX), and on one probe turn the model's edit dropped
                                       statements wholesale (`d7`/`d8` vanished) — that's the known "keep
                                       edits surgical" J3 guidance task, upstream of the renderer, and worth
                                       keeping on the radar there.
